'otp':\n            speak('Please enter the 6-digit verification code.');\n            break;\n          case 'profile':\n            speak('Tell me your company name and what products you sell.');\n            break;\n          case 'upload':\n            speak('Now upload your product catalog. You can upload PDFs, images, and more.');\n            break;\n          case 'complete':\n            saveVendor();\n            speak('Congratulations! Your vendor profile is complete!');\n            break;\n        }\n      }, 300);\n    }\n  }, [step]);\n\n  const goBack = useCallback(() => {\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx > 0) {\n      setStep(STEPS[idx - 1]);\n    } else {\n      onClose();\n    }\n  }, [step, onClose]);\n\n  // VOICE COMMAND HANDLER - The main brain\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase().trim();\n    console.log(`\ud83c\udfa4 [${step}] Voice:`, lower);\n\n    // Extract digits\n    const digits = extractDigits(lower);\n\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    // PHONE STEP\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    if (step === 'phone' && digits.length > 0) {\n      const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\n      typeIntoField(phoneInputRef, newPhone, setPhone);\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) {\n        speak('Phone complete! Say next or send to continue.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    // OTP STEP\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\n      typeIntoField(otpInputRef, newOtp, setOtp);\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) {\n        speak('Code complete! Say verify to continue.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    // PROFILE STEP\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    if (step === 'profile') {\n      // Company name extraction\n      const companyPatterns = [\n        /(?:my company is|company name is|company is|we are|i'm from|this is|called)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\s+and|\\s+we|\\.|,|$)/i,\n        /^(.+?)\\s+(?:inc|llc|corp|company|co\\b|limited)/i\n      ];\n      \n      for (const pattern of companyPatterns) {\n        const match = text.match(pattern);\n        if (match && match[1] && match[1].length > 2 && !companyName) {\n          const name = match[1].trim().replace(/^(called|named)\\s+/i, '');\n          typeIntoField(companyInputRef, name, setCompanyName);\n          speak(`Got it, ${name}!`);\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Description extraction\n      const descPatterns = [\n        /(?:we sell|we offer|we make|we provide|we specialize in|dealing in|we deal in|products are|selling)\\s+(.+)/i,\n        /(?:our products include|our services include)\\s+(.+)/i\n      ];\n      \n      for (const pattern of descPatterns) {\n        const match = text.match(pattern);\n        if (match && match[1] && match[1].length > 3) {\n          typeIntoField(descriptionRef, match[1].trim(), setDescription);\n          speak('Got your description!');\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Beautify command\n      if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance') || lower.includes('improve')) {\n        handleBeautify();\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    // NAVIGATION COMMANDS (work on all steps)\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    if (lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue') || lower.includes('proceed') || \n        lower.includes('send') || lower.includes('verify') || lower.includes('save')) {\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) {\n        speak('Sending verification code.');\n        goNext();\n      } else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) {\n        speak('Verifying code.');\n        goNext();\n      } else if (step === 'profile' && companyName.trim() && description.trim()) {\n        speak('Saving profile.');\n        goNext();\n      } else if (step === 'upload') {\n        speak('Completing setup.');\n        goNext();\n      } else {\n        speak('Please complete the current field first.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (lower.includes('back') || lower.includes('previous') || lower.includes('go back')) {\n      speak('Going back.');\n      goBack();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (lower.includes('clear') || lower.includes('reset') || lower.includes('start over')) {\n      if (step === 'phone') {\n        setPhone('');\n        if (phoneInputRef.current) phoneInputRef.current.value = '';\n      } else if (step === 'otp') {\n        setOtp('');\n        if (otpInputRef.current) otpInputRef.current.value = '';\n      }\n      speak('Cleared.');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (lower.includes('skip')) {\n      if (step === 'upload') {\n        speak('Skipping upload.');\n        goNext();\n      }\n    }\n  }, [step, phone, otp, companyName, description, goNext, goBack, speak]);\n\n  // Beautify\n  const handleBeautify = async () => {\n    if (!description.trim()) {\n      speak('Please enter a description first.');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    setIsBeautifying(true);\n    speak('Enhancing your description...');\n\n    try {\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/beautify', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ text: description, type: 'vendor', companyName })\n      });\n\n      const data = await response.json();\n      if (data.beautified) {\n        await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, data.beautified, setDescription);\n        speak('Description enhanced beautifully!');\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      const enhanced = `${companyName || 'Our company'} is a premier supplier of ${description}. We offer high-quality products with exceptional service.`;\n      await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, enhanced, setDescription);\n      speak('Description enhanced!');\n    } finally {\n      setIsBeautifying(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Save vendor\n  const saveVendor = async () => {\n    try {\n      await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          phone,\n          companyName,\n          description,\n          files: uploadedFiles.map(f => ({ name: f.file?.name, category: f.category, url: f.url }))\n        })\n      });\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Save error:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => {\n    if (p.length <= 3) return p;\n    if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`;\n    return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\n  };\n\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n\n  const getWelcome = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone': return 'Welcome vendor! Say your phone number digit by digit.';\n      case 'otp': return 'Enter the 6-digit verification code.';\n      case 'profile': return 'Tell me your company name and what products you sell.';\n      case 'upload': return 'Upload your product catalog. PDFs, images, CAD files accepted.';\n      default: return '';\n    }\n  };\n\n  const getHints = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone': return ['seven zero three...', 'next', 'clear'];\n      case 'otp': return ['one two three four five six', 'verify'];\n      case 'profile': return ['My company is ABC Corp', 'We sell flooring materials', 'beautify'];\n      case 'upload': return ['skip', 'next'];\n      default: return [];\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Render each step\n  const renderStep = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone':\n        return (\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n              <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\ud83d\udce6</span>\n              <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0 5px' }}>Vendor Phone</h3>\n              <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Say digits: \"seven zero three...\"</p>\n            </div>\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>+1</span>\n              <input\n                ref={phoneInputRef}\n                type=\"tel\"\n                value={formatPhone(phone)}\n                onChange={e => setPhone(e.target.value.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10))}\n                placeholder=\"000-000-0000\"\n                style={{\n                  padding: '16px 20px',\n                  fontSize: '1.5em',\n                  fontFamily: 'monospace',\n                  background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n                  border: `2px solid ${phone.length === 10 ? '#10b981' : THEME.accent}40`,\n                  borderRadius: 12,\n                  color: '#fff',\n                  textAlign: 'center',\n                  width: 220,\n                  outline: 'none'\n                }}\n              />\n            </div>\n            <button\n              onClick={goNext}\n              disabled={phone.length !== 10}\n              style={{\n                padding: '14px 40px',\n                background: phone.length === 10 ? THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n                border: 'none',\n                borderRadius: 30,\n                color: phone.length === 10 ? '#000' : '#666',\n                fontWeight: 600,\n                cursor: phone.length === 10 ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',\n                alignSelf: 'center'\n              }}\n            >\n              Send OTP \u2192\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        );\n\n      case 'otp':\n        return (\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n              <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\ud83d\udd10</span>\n              <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0 5px' }}>Verification Code</h3>\n              <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Say digits: \"one two three...\"</p>\n            </div>\n            <input\n              ref={otpInputRef}\n              type=\"text\"\n              value={otp}\n              onChange={e => setOtp(e.target.value.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 6))}\n              placeholder=\"000000\"\n              maxLength={6}\n              style={{\n                padding: '16px 20px',\n                fontSize: '2em',\n                fontFamily: 'monospace',\n                background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n                border: `2px solid ${otp.length === 6 ? '#10b981' : THEME.accent}40`,\n                borderRadius: 12,\n                color: '#fff',\n                textAlign: 'center',\n                width: 200,\n                letterSpacing: 10,\n                alignSelf: 'center',\n                outline: 'none'\n              }}\n            />\n            <button\n              onClick={goNext}\n              disabled={otp.length !== 6}\n              style={{\n                padding: '14px 40px',\n                background: otp.length === 6 ? THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n                border: 'none',\n                borderRadius: 30,\n                color: otp.length === 6 ? '#000' : '#666',\n                fontWeight: 600,\n                cursor: otp.length === 6 ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',\n                alignSelf: 'center'\n              }}\n            >\n              Verify \u2192\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        );\n\n      case 'profile':\n        return (\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n              <span style={{ fontSize: '2.5em' }}>\ud83c\udfe2</span>\n              <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0 5px' }}>Company Profile</h3>\n              <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Say \"My company is...\" and \"We sell...\"</p>\n            </div>\n            <input\n              ref={companyInputRef}\n              type=\"text\"\n              value={companyName}\n              onChange={e => setCompanyName(e.target.value)}\n              placeholder=\"Company Name\"\n              style={{\n                padding: '14px 18px',\n                background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n                border: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}40`,\n                borderRadius: 10,\n                color: '#fff',\n                fontSize: '1em',\n                outline: 'none'\n              }}\n            />\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n              <label style={{ color: '#ccc', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>Products/Services</label>\n              <button\n                onClick={handleBeautify}\n                disabled={isBeautifying || !description.trim()}\n                style={{\n                  padding: '6px 14px',\n                  borderRadius: 15,\n                  border: 'none',\n                  background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #8b5cf6, #6366f1)',\n                  color: '#fff',\n                  fontSize: '0.8em',\n                  cursor: 'pointer',\n                  opacity: !description.trim() ? 0.5 : 1\n                }}\n              >\n                {isBeautifying ? '\u23f3' : '\u2728'} Beautify\n              </button>\n            </div>\n            <textarea\n              ref={descriptionRef}\n              value={description}\n              onChange={e => setDescription(e.target.value)}\n              placeholder=\"Describe your products...\"\n              rows={4}\n              style={{\n                padding: '14px 18px',\n                background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n                border: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}40`,\n                borderRadius: 10,\n                color: '#fff',\n                fontSize: '1em',\n                resize: 'vertical',\n                fontFamily: 'inherit',\n                outline: 'none'\n              }}\n            />\n            <button\n              onClick={goNext}\n              disabled={!companyName.trim() || !description.trim()}\n              style={{\n                padding: '14px 40px',\n                background: (companyName.trim() && description.trim()) ? THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n                border: 'none',\n                borderRadius: 30,\n                color: (companyName.trim() && description.trim()) ? '#000' : '#666',\n                fontWeight: 600,\n                cursor: (companyName.trim() && description.trim()) ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',\n                alignSelf: 'center'\n              }}\n            >\n              Save Profile \u2192\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        );\n\n      case 'upload':\n        return (\n          <MultiFormatUploader\n            userType=\"vendor\"\n            accentColor={THEME.accent}\n            speak={speak}\n            onFilesUploaded={setUploadedFiles}\n            onAllComplete={() => goNext()}\n          />\n        );\n\n      case 'complete':\n        return (\n          <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 40 }}>\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83c\udf89</span>\n            <h2 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '20px 0 10px' }}>Setup Complete!</h2>\n            <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: 30 }}>\n              Your vendor profile is ready. Products will be processed shortly.\n            </p>\n            <button\n              onClick={onClose}\n              style={{\n                padding: '14px 40px',\n                background: THEME.accent,\n                border: 'none',\n                borderRadius: 30,\n                color: '#000',\n                fontWeight: 600,\n                cursor: 'pointer'\n              }}\n            >\n              View Dashboard \u2192\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        );\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      position: 'fixed',\n      inset: 0,\n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)',\n      zIndex: 10000,\n      display: 'flex',\n      justifyContent: 'center',\n      alignItems: 'center',\n      padding: 20\n    }}>\n      <div style={{\n        background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.primary}, ${THEME.secondary})`,\n        borderRadius: 20,\n        width: '100%',\n        maxWidth: 650,\n        maxHeight: '90vh',\n        overflow: 'hidden',\n        border: `2px solid ${THEME.accent}40`,\n        boxShadow: '0 25px 80px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)'\n      }}>\n        {/* Header */}\n        <div style={{\n          padding: '16px 24px',\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n          borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}30`,\n          display: 'flex',\n          justifyContent: 'space-between',\n          alignItems: 'center'\n        }}>\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 14 }}>\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\ud83d\udce6</span>\n            <div>\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length}</span>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          <button\n            onClick={onClose}\n            style={{\n              background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n              border: 'none',\n              color: '#fff',\n              width: 36,\n              height: 36,\n              borderRadius: '50%',\n              cursor: 'pointer',\n              fontSize: '1.1em'\n            }}\n          >\n            \u2715\n          </button>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Progress Bar */}\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: 4, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\n          {STEPS.map((_, i) => (\n            <div\n              key={i}\n              style={{\n                flex: 1,\n                height: 4,\n                borderRadius: 2,\n                background: i <= stepIndex ? THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)',\n                transition: 'background 0.3s'\n              }}\n            />\n          ))}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Back Button */}\n        {step !== 'complete' && (\n          <div style={{ padding: '12px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\n            <button\n              onClick={goBack}\n              style={{\n                padding: '6px 14px',\n                background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n                border: 'none',\n                color: '#fff',\n                borderRadius: 15,\n                cursor: 'pointer',\n                fontSize: '0.9em'\n              }}\n            >\n              \u2190 Back\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        )}\n\n        {/* Step Content */}\n        <div style={{ padding: 24, overflow: 'auto', maxHeight: 'calc(90vh - 280px)' }}>\n          {renderStep()}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Agentic Bar - KEY: stepKey forces proper restart */}\n        {step !== 'complete' && (\n          <div style={{ padding: '0 24px 24px' }}>\n            <UniversalAgenticBar\n              ref={agenticBarRef}\n              welcomeMessage={getWelcome()}\n              hints={getHints()}\n              onCommand={handleVoiceCommand}\n              autoStart={true}\n              accentColor={THEME.accent}\n              context={step}\n += next + next; i++; continue; }\n      }\n      if (word === 'triple' && i + 1 < words.length) {\n        const next = WORD_TO_DIGIT[words[i + 1]] || words[i + 1].replace(/\\D/g, '');\n        if (next.length === 1) { result += next + next + next; i++; continue; }\n      }\n      if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) result += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n      else result += word.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    }\n    return result;\n  };\n\n  // Check for navigation keywords\n  const isNextCommand = (text: string) => NAV_NEXT.some(k => text.toLowerCase().includes(k));\n  const isBackCommand = (text: string) => NAV_BACK.some(k => text.toLowerCase().includes(k));\n\n  const goNext = useCallback(() => {\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx < STEPS.length - 1) {\n      const nextStep = STEPS[idx + 1];\n      setStep(nextStep);\n      \n      setTimeout(() => {\n        switch (nextStep) {\n          case 'otp':\n            speak('Great! Now enter the 6-digit verification code.');\n            pointTo('otp-input');\n            break;\n          case 'company':\n            speak('What is your company name?');\n            pointTo('company-input');\n            break;\n          case 'description':\n            speak('Tell me what products you sell. Say beautify when done to enhance it.');\n            pointTo('description-input');\n            break;\n          case 'upload':\n            speak('Now lets upload your product catalog. Say upload PDF or click the upload area.');\n            pointTo('upload-area');\n            break;\n          case 'processing':\n            startProcessing();\n            break;\n          case 'complete':\n            speak('Congratulations! Your vendor profile is complete and products are published!');\n            break;\n        }\n      }, 300);\n    }\n  }, [step, speak, pointTo]);\n\n  const goBack = useCallback(() => {\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx > 0) setStep(STEPS[idx - 1]);\n    else onClose();\n  }, [step, onClose]);\n\n  // PDF Processing - 5 Steps\n  const startProcessing = async () => {\n    const steps = [\n      { msg: 'Uploading your catalog to secure storage...', delay: 1500 },\n      { msg: 'Wow! Extracting images from your PDF... This looks great!', delay: 2000 },\n      { msg: 'Amazing! Analyzing products and descriptions...', delay: 2500 },\n      { msg: 'Creating smart search vectors for your products...', delay: 2000 },\n      { msg: 'Publishing to your product catalog... Almost done!', delay: 1500 },\n    ];\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {\n      setProcessingStep(i + 1);\n      speak(steps[i].msg);\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, steps[i].delay));\n    }\n\n    // Simulate extracted products\n    setExtractedProducts([\n      { name: 'Premium Hardwood Flooring', price: 89.99 },\n      { name: 'Ceramic Wall Tiles', price: 45.00 },\n      { name: 'Luxury Vinyl Plank', price: 65.50 },\n    ]);\n\n    await saveVendor();\n    goNext();\n  };\n\n  // Voice command handler\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase().trim();\n    console.log(`\ud83c\udfa4 [${step}]`, lower);\n\n    // NAVIGATION - works on all steps\n    if (isNextCommand(lower)) {\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) { speak('Sending verification code.'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) { speak('Verifying.'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'company' && companyName.trim()) { speak('Got it!'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'description' && description.trim()) { speak('Saving your description.'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'upload') { speak('Processing your catalog.'); goNext(); }\n      else speak('Please complete this field first.');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (isBackCommand(lower)) { speak('Going back.'); goBack(); return; }\n\n    // PHONE\n    if (step === 'phone') {\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\n        const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\n        typeIntoField(phoneInputRef, newPhone, setPhone);\n        if (newPhone.length === 10) speak('Phone complete! Say next to continue.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // OTP\n    if (step === 'otp') {\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\n        const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\n        typeIntoField(otpInputRef, newOtp, setOtp);\n        if (newOtp.length === 6) speak('Code complete! Say verify to continue.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // COMPANY NAME\n    if (step === 'company') {\n      // Remove filler words and use whatever they say\n      const cleanedName = text\n        .replace(/^(my company is|company name is|we are|i'm from|this is|it's called|called)\\s*/i, '')\n        .replace(/\\s+(inc|llc|corp|company|co)\\.?$/i, ' $1')\n        .trim();\n      \n      if (cleanedName.length > 1) {\n        typeIntoField(companyInputRef, cleanedName, setCompanyName);\n        speak(`Got it, ${cleanedName}! Say next when ready.`);\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // DESCRIPTION\n    if (step === 'description') {\n      // Beautify command\n      if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance') || lower.includes('improve')) {\n        handleBeautify();\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // Clear command\n      if (lower.includes('clear') || lower.includes('reset')) {\n        setDescription('');\n        if (descriptionRef.current) descriptionRef.current.value = '';\n        speak('Cleared. Tell me about your products.');\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // Add to description\n      const cleanedDesc = text\n        .replace(/^(we sell|we offer|we make|we provide|we specialize in|we deal in|our products are|products include)\\s*/i, '')\n        .trim();\n      \n      if (cleanedDesc.length > 2) {\n        const newDesc = description ? `${description} ${cleanedDesc}` : cleanedDesc;\n        typeIntoField(descriptionRef, newDesc, setDescription);\n        speak('Got it! Say beautify to enhance, or next to continue.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // UPLOAD\n    if (step === 'upload') {\n      if (lower.includes('upload') || lower.includes('pdf') || lower.includes('catalog') || lower.includes('open')) {\n        speak('Opening file selector. Choose your PDF from downloads.');\n        fileInputRef.current?.click();\n        return;\n      }\n      if (lower.includes('skip')) {\n        speak('Skipping upload.');\n        goNext();\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n  }, [step, phone, otp, companyName, description, goNext, goBack, speak, pointTo]);\n\n  // Beautify\n  const handleBeautify = async () => {\n    if (!description.trim()) { speak('Please add a description first.'); return; }\n    setIsBeautifying(true);\n    speak('Beautifying your description... This is what you described, let me make it shine!');\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/beautify', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ text: description, type: 'vendor', companyName })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (data.beautified) {\n        await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, data.beautified, setDescription);\n        speak('Beautiful! Here is your enhanced description. Say next when ready.');\n      }\n    } catch {\n      const enhanced = `${companyName || 'We'} offer premium ${description}. Our products feature exceptional quality, competitive pricing, and outstanding customer service.`;\n      await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, enhanced, setDescription);\n      speak('Enhanced! Say next to continue.');\n    }\n    setIsBeautifying(false);\n  };\n\n  // Handle file upload\n  const handleFileUpload = async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n    const file = e.target.files?.[0];\n    if (!file) return;\n    \n    speak(`Great! You selected ${file.name}. Processing now.`);\n    setUploadedFiles([{ file, category: 'catalog' }]);\n    \n    // Go to processing\n    goNext();\n  };\n\n  // Save vendor\n  const saveVendor = async () => {\n    try {\n      await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ phone, companyName, description, files: uploadedFiles.map(f => f.file?.name) })\n      });\n    } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => {\n    if (p.length <= 3) return p;\n    if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`;\n    return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\n  };\n\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n\n  const getWelcome = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone': return 'Welcome vendor! Say your phone number digit by digit.';\n      case 'otp': return 'Say the 6-digit code.';\n      case 'company': return 'What is your company name?';\n      case 'description': return 'What products do you sell? Say beautify when done.';\n      case 'upload': return 'Say upload PDF to select your catalog.';\n      default: return '';\n    }\n  };\n\n  const getHints = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone': return ['seven zero three...', 'next'];\n      case 'otp': return ['one two three...', 'verify'];\n      case 'company': return ['ABC Materials', 'next'];\n      case 'description': return ['flooring and tiles', 'beautify', 'next'];\n      case 'upload': return ['upload PDF', 'skip'];\n      default: return [];\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Render steps\n  const renderStep = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone':\n        return (\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n              <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\ud83d\udce6</span>\n              <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0' }}>Vendor Phone</h3>\n              <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Say: \"seven zero three...\"</p>\n            </div>\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\n              <span style={{ color: '#888' }}>+1</span>\n              <input id=\"phone-input\" ref={phoneInputRef} type=\"tel\" value={formatPhone(phone)} onChange={e => setPhone(e.target.value.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10))} placeholder=\"000-000-0000\" style={{ padding: '16px 20px', fontSize: '1.5em', fontFamily: 'monospace', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', border: `2px solid ${phone.length === 10 ? {\n      if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) result += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n      else result += word.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    }\n    return result;\n  };\n\n  const isNextCommand = (t: string) => NAV_NEXT.some(k => t.toLowerCase().includes(k));\n  const isBackCommand = (t: string) => NAV_BACK.some(k => t.toLowerCase().includes(k));\n\n  const goNext = useCallback(() => {\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx < STEPS.length - 1) {\n      const nextStep = STEPS[idx + 1];\n      setStep(nextStep);\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        if (nextStep === 'otp') speak('Enter the 6-digit code.');\n        else if (nextStep === 'license') speak('What is your real estate license number? Say the state name too.');\n        else if (nextStep === 'company') speak('What agency or brokerage are you with?');\n        else if (nextStep === 'description') speak('What do you specialize in? Luxury homes, first-time buyers?');\n        else if (nextStep === 'upload') speak('Upload property listings or photos.');\n        else if (nextStep === 'processing') startProcessing();\n        else if (nextStep === 'complete') speak('Your agent profile is complete!');\n      }, 300);\n    }\n  }, [step, speak]);\n\n  const goBack = useCallback(() => {\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx > 0) setStep(STEPS[idx - 1]);\n    else onClose();\n  }, [step, onClose]);\n\n  const startProcessing = async () => {\n    const steps = ['Uploading listings...', 'Analyzing photos...', 'Extracting property details...', 'Creating search vectors...', 'Publishing profile...'];\n    for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {\n      setProcessingStep(i + 1);\n      speak(steps[i]);\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1800));\n    }\n    await saveAgent();\n    goNext();\n  };\n\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase().trim();\n\n    if (isNextCommand(lower)) {\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) { speak('Sending code.'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) { speak('Verifying.'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'license' && license && licenseState) { speak('Got it!'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'company' && companyName.trim()) { speak('Got it!'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'description' && description.trim()) { speak('Saving.'); goNext(); }\n      else if (step === 'upload') { speak('Processing.'); goNext(); }\n      else speak('Please complete this field first.');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (isBackCommand(lower)) { speak('Going back.'); goBack(); return; }\n\n    if (step === 'phone') {\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\n        const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\n        typeIntoField(phoneInputRef, newPhone, setPhone);\n        if (newPhone.length === 10) speak('Phone complete! Say next.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'otp') {\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\n        const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\n        typeIntoField(otpInputRef, newOtp, setOtp);\n        if (newOtp.length === 6) speak('Code complete! Say verify.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'license') {\n      // Check for state name\n      for (const state of STATES) {\n        if (lower.includes(state.toLowerCase())) {\n          setLicenseState(state);\n          speak(`State set to ${state}.`);\n          break;\n        }\n      }\n      // Check for license number\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\n        const newLicense = (license + digits).slice(0, 12);\n        typeIntoField(licenseInputRef, newLicense, setLicense);\n      }\n      // Also accept alphanumeric\n      const alphaNum = text.match(/[A-Za-z0-9]{5,12}/);\n      if (alphaNum && !license) {\n        typeIntoField(licenseInputRef, alphaNum[0].toUpperCase(), setLicense);\n        speak('Got your license number.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'company') {\n      const cleanedName = text.replace(/^(my agency is|i work at|i'm with|brokerage is|agency is)\\s*/i, '').trim();\n      if (cleanedName.length > 1) {\n        typeIntoField(companyInputRef, cleanedName, setCompanyName);\n        speak(`Got it, ${cleanedName}! Say next.`);\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'description') {\n      if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance')) { handleBeautify(); return; }\n      const cleanedDesc = text.replace(/^(i specialize in|i focus on|i help with|my specialty is)\\s*/i, '').trim();\n      if (cleanedDesc.length > 2) {\n        const newDesc = description ? `${description} ${cleanedDesc}` : cleanedDesc;\n        typeIntoField(descriptionRef, newDesc, setDescription);\n        speak('Got it! Say beautify or next.');\n      }\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'upload') {\n      if (lower.includes('upload') || lower.includes('listing')) { fileInputRef.current?.click(); return; }\n      if (lower.includes('skip')) { speak('Skipping.'); goNext(); }\n    }\n  }, [step, phone, otp, license, licenseState, companyName, description, goNext, goBack, speak]);\n\n  const handleBeautify = async () => {\n    if (!description.trim()) { speak('Add a description first.'); return; }\n    setIsBeautifying(true);\n    speak('Enhancing your agent profile...');\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/beautify', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ text: description, type: 'agent', companyName })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (data.beautified) await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, data.beautified, setDescription);\n    } catch {\n      const enhanced = `As a licensed real estate professional with ${companyName}, I specialize in ${description}. I provide expert guidance to help clients achieve their property goals.`;\n      await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, enhanced, setDescription);\n    }\n    speak('Enhanced! Say next.');\n    setIsBeautifying(false);\n  };\n\n  const handleFileUpload = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n    const file = e.target.files?.[0];\n    if (file) { speak(`Selected ${file.name}. Processing.`); goNext(); }\n  };\n\n  const saveAgent = async () => {\n    try {\n      await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/agents', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ phone, license, licenseState, companyName, description })\n      });\n    } catch (e) {}\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => p.length <= 3 ? p : p.length <= 6 ? `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}` : `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n\n  const getWelcome = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone': return 'Welcome agent! words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n    for (let i = 0; i < words.length; i++) {\\n      const word = words[i];\\n      if (word === 'double' && i + 1 < words.length) {\\n        const next = WORD_TO_DIGIT[words[i + 1]] || words[i + 1].replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n        if (next.length === 1) { result += next + next; i++; continue; }\\n      }\\n      if (word === 'triple' && i + 1 < words.length) {\\n        const next = WORD_TO_DIGIT[words[i + 1]] || words[i + 1].replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n        if (next.length === 1) { result += next + next + next; i++; continue; }\\n      }\\n      if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) result += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n      else result += word.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    }\\n    return result;\\n  };\\n\\n  // Check for navigation keywords\\n  const Your vendor profile is complete and products are published!');\\n            break;\\n        }\\n      }, 300);\\n    }\\n  }, [step, speak, pointTo]);\\n\\n  const goBack = useCallback(() => {\\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n    if (idx > 0) setStep(STEPS[idx - 1]);\\n    else onClose();\\n  }, [step, onClose]);\\n\\n  // PDF Processing - 5 Steps\\n  const startProcessing = async () => {\\n    const steps = [\\n      { msg: 'Uploading your catalog to secure storage...', delay: 1500 },\\n      { msg: 'Wow! Almost done!', delay: 1500 },\\n    ];\\n\\n    for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {\\n      setProcessingStep(i + 1);\\n      speak(steps[i].msg);\\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, steps[i].delay));\\n    }\\n\\n    // Simulate extracted products\\n    setExtractedProducts([\\n      { name: 'Premium Hardwood Flooring', price: 89.99 },\\n      { name: 'Ceramic Wall Tiles', price: 45.00 },\\n      { name: 'Luxury Vinyl Plank', price: 65.50 },\\n    ]);\\n\\n    await saveVendor();\\n    goNext();\\n  };\\n\\n  // Voice command handler\\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase().trim();\\n    console.log(`\\ud83c\\udfa4 [${step}]`, lower);\\n\\n    // NAVIGATION - works on all steps\\n    if (isNextCommand(lower)) {\\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) { speak('Sending verification code.'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) { speak('Verifying.'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'company' && companyName.trim()) { speak('Got it!'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'description' && description.trim()) { speak('Saving your description.'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'upload') { speak('Processing your catalog.'); goNext(); }\\n      else speak('Please complete this field first.');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    if (isBackCommand(lower)) { speak('Going back.'); goBack(); return; }\\n\\n    // PHONE\\n    if (step === 'phone') {\\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\\n        const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n        typeIntoField(phoneInputRef, newPhone, setPhone);\\n        if (newPhone.length === 10) speak('Phone complete! STEPS = ['phone', 'otp', 'license', 'company', 'description', 'upload', 'processing', 'complete'] as const;\\ntype Step = typeof STEPS[number];\\n\\nconst THEME = { primary: '#1a1a2e', secondary: '#16213e', accent: '#10b981' };\\n\\nconst STATES = ['Alabama','Alaska','Arizona','Arkansas','California','Colorado','Connecticut','Delaware','Florida','Georgia','Hawaii','Idaho','Illinois','Indiana','Iowa','Kansas','Kentucky','Louisiana','Maine','Maryland','Massachusetts','Michigan','Minnesota','Mississippi','Missouri','Montana','Nebraska','Nevada','New Hampshire','New Jersey','New Mexico','New York','North Carolina','North Dakota','Ohio','Oklahoma','Oregon','Pennsylvania','Rhode Island','South Carolina','South Dakota','Tennessee','Texas','Utah','Vermont','Virginia','Washington','West Virginia','Wisconsin','Wyoming'];\\n\\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4',\\n  'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9',\\n};\\n\\nconst NAV_NEXT = ['next', 'done', 'continue', 'proceed', 'verify', 'save'];\\nconst NAV_BACK = ['back', 'previous', 'go back'];\\n\\nconst AgentFlow: React.FC<AgentFlowProps> = ({ onClose }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');\\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\\n  const [license, setLicense] = useState('');\\n  const [licenseState, setLicenseState] = useState('');\\n  const [companyName, setCompanyName] = useState('');\\n  const [description, setDescription] = useState('');\\n  const [isBeautifying, setIsBeautifying] = useState(false);\\n  const [processingStep, setProcessingStep] = useState(0);\\n\\n  const agenticBarRef = useRef<AgenticBarRef>(null);\\n  const phoneInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n  const otpInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n  const licenseInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n  const companyInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n  const descriptionRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);\\n  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => agenticBarRef.current?.speak(text), []);\\n\\n  const typeIntoField = async (ref: React.RefObject<any>, value: string, setter: React.Dispatch<React.SetStateAction<string>>) => {\\n    for (let i = 0; i <= value.length; i++) {\\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 25));\\n      setter(value.slice(0, i));\\n      if (ref.current) ref.current.value = value.slice(0, i);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n    let result = '';\\n    for (const word of text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/)) {\\n      if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) result += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n      else result += word.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    }\\n    return result;\\n  };\\n\\n  const isNextCommand = (t: string) => NAV_NEXT.some(k => t.toLowerCase().includes(k));\\n  const isBackCommand = (t: string) => NAV_BACK.some(k => t.toLowerCase().includes(k));\\n\\n  const goNext = useCallback(() => {\\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n    if (idx < STEPS.length - 1) {\\n      const nextStep = STEPS[idx + 1];\\n      setStep(nextStep);\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        if (nextStep === 'otp') speak('Enter the 6-digit code.');\\n        else if (nextStep === 'license') speak('What is your real estate license number? Say the state name too.');\\n        else if (nextStep === 'company') speak('What agency or brokerage are you with?');\\n        else if (nextStep === 'description') speak('What do you specialize in? Luxury homes, first-time buyers?');\\n        else if (nextStep === 'upload') speak('Upload property listings or photos.');\\n        else if (nextStep === 'processing') startProcessing();\\n        else if (nextStep === 'complete') speak('Your agent profile is complete!');\\n      }, 300);\\n    }\\n  }, [step, speak]);\\n\\n  const goBack = useCallback(() => {\\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n    if (idx > 0) setStep(STEPS[idx - 1]);\\n    else onClose();\\n  }, [step, onClose]);\\n\\n  const startProcessing = async () => {\\n    const steps = ['Uploading listings...', 'Analyzing photos...', 'Extracting property details...', 'Creating search vectors...', 'Publishing profile...'];\\n    for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {\\n      setProcessingStep(i + 1);\\n      speak(steps[i]);\\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1800));\\n    }\\n    await saveAgent();\\n    goNext();\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase().trim();\\n\\n    if (isNextCommand(lower)) {\\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) { speak('Sending code.'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) { speak('Verifying.'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'license' && license && licenseState) { speak('Got it!'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'company' && companyName.trim()) { speak('Got it!'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'description' && description.trim()) { speak('Saving.'); goNext(); }\\n      else if (step === 'upload') { speak('Processing.'); goNext(); }\\n      else speak('Please complete this field first.');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (isBackCommand(lower)) { speak('Going back.'); goBack(); return; }\\n\\n    if (step === 'phone') {\\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\\n        const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n        typeIntoField(phoneInputRef, newPhone, setPhone);\\n        if (newPhone.length === 10) speak('Phone complete! Say next.');\\n      }\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'otp') {\\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\\n        const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\\n        typeIntoField(otpInputRef, newOtp, setOtp);\\n        if (newOtp.length === 6) speak('Code complete! Say verify.');\\n      }\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'license') {\\n      // Check for state name\\n      for (const state of STATES) {\\n        if (lower.includes(state.toLowerCase())) {\\n          setLicenseState(state);\\n          speak(`State set to ${state}.`);\\n          break;\\n        }\\n      }\\n      // Check for license number\\n      const digits = extractDigits(lower);\\n      if (digits.length > 0) {\\n        const newLicense = (license + digits).slice(0, 12);\\n        typeIntoField(licenseInputRef, newLicense, setLicense);\\n      }\\n      // Also accept alphanumeric\\n      const alphaNum = text.match(/[A-Za-z0-9]{5,12}/);\\n      if (alphaNum && !license) {\\n        typeIntoField(licenseInputRef, alphaNum[0].toUpperCase(), setLicense);\\n        speak('Got your license number.');\\n      }\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'company') {\\n      const cleanedName = text.replace(/^(my agency is|i work at|i'm with|brokerage is|agency is)\\\\s*/i, '').trim();\\n      if (cleanedName.length > 1) {\\n        typeIntoField(companyInputRef, cleanedName, setCompanyName);\\n        speak(`Got it, ${cleanedName}! Say next.`);\\n      }\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'description') {\\n      if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance')) { handleBeautify(); return; }\\n      const cleanedDesc = text.replace(/^(i specialize in|i focus on|i help with|my specialty is)\\\\s*/i, '').trim();\\n      if (cleanedDesc.length > 2) {\\n        const newDesc = description ? `${description} ${cleanedDesc}` : cleanedDesc;\\n        typeIntoField(descriptionRef, newDesc, setDescription);\\n        speak('Got it! Say beautify or next.');\\n      }\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'upload') {\\n      if (lower.includes('upload') || lower.includes('listing')) { fileInputRef.current?.click(); return; }\\n      if (lower.includes('skip')) { speak('Skipping.'); goNext(); }\\n    }\\n  }, [step, phone, otp, license, licenseState, companyName, description, goNext, goBack, speak]);\\n\\n  const handleBeautify = async () => {\\n    if (!description.trim()) { speak('Add a description first.'); return; }\\n    setIsBeautifying(true);\\n    speak('Enhancing your agent profile...');\\n    try {\\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/beautify', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({ text: description, type: 'agent', companyName })\\n      });\\n      const data = await res.json();\\n      if (data.beautified) await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, data.beautified, setDescription);\\n    } catch {\\n      const enhanced = `As a licensed real estate professional with ${companyName}, I specialize in ${description}. I provide expert guidance to help clients achieve their property goals.`;\\n      await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, enhanced, setDescription);\\n    }\\n    speak('Enhanced! Say next.');\\n    setIsBeautifying(false);\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleFileUpload = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\\n    const file = e.target.files?.[0];\\n    if (file) { speak(`Selected ${file.name}. Processing.`); goNext(); }\\n  };\\n\\n  const saveAgent = async () => {\\n    try {\\n      await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/agents', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({ phone, license, licenseState, companyName, description })\\n      });\\n    } catch (e) {}\\n  };\\n\\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => p.length <= 3 ? p : p.length <= 6 ? `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}` : `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n\\n  const getWelcome = () => {\\n    switch (step) {\\n      case 'phone': return 'Welcome agent! Say your phone number.';\\n      case 'otp': return 'Say the 6-digit code.';\\n      case 'license': return 'What is your license number and state?';\\n      case 'company': return 'What agency are you with?';\\n      case 'description': return 'What do you specialize in?';\\n      case 'upload': return 'Upload your listings.';\\n      default: return '';\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const getHints = () => {\\n    switch (step) {\\n      case 'phone': return ['seven zero three...', 'next'];\\n      case 'otp': return ['one two three...', 'verify'];\\n      case 'license': return ['Texas', 'California', 'next'];\\n      case 'company': return ['RE/MAX', 'Keller Williams', 'next'];\\n      case 'description': return ['luxury homes', 'beautify', 'next'];\\n      case 'upload': return ['upload listings', 'skip'];\\n      default: return [];\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const renderStep = () => {\\n    switch (step) {\\n      case 'phone':\\n        return (\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}><span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\\ud83c\\udfe0</span><h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0' }}>Agent Phone</h3></div>\\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}><span style={{ color: '#888' }}>+1</span><input ref={phoneInputRef} type=\\\"tel\\\" value={formatPhone(phone)} onChange={e => setPhone(e.target.value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10))} placeholder=\\\"000-000-0000\\\" style={{ padding: '16px 20px', fontSize: '1.5em', fontFamily: 'monospace', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', border: `2px solid ${THEME.accent}40`, borderRadius: 12, color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center', width: 220 }} /></div>\\n            <button onClick={goNext} disabled={phone.length !== 10} style={{ padding: '14px 40px', background: phone.length === 10 ? '#fff' : '#666' }}>{['Uploading', 'Analyzing', 'Extracting', 'Vectorizing', 'Publishing'][i-1]}</span>\\n              </div>\\n            ))}\\n          </div>\\n        );\\n      case 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', zIndex: 10000, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', padding: 20 }}>\\n      <div style={{ background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.primary}, THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' }} />))}</div>\\n        {!['processing', 'complete'].includes(step) && (<div style={{ padding: '12px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}><button
